Approved — proceed with Phase 3.This scope is correct.The next priority is to complete the first true gameplay loop:exploration -> wild encounter -> battle -> capture or win -> return to explorationPlease enforce the following constraints during implementation:1. Keep the scope small- Only implement the first battle loop for wild encounters- Do not add advanced quest UI, codex polish, or complex evolution yet- Make the loop stable first2. Preserve Phaser 3 + JavaScript- Do not switch to TypeScript- Do not reintroduce React gameplay components- Keep the Phaser scene structure clean3. Data must be separated from scene codeCreate and use separate files for:- creatures.js- skills.js- encounters.js- battleSystem.jsDo not hardcode all creature and battle data directly inside BattleScene.4. Starter preservation is mandatoryThe selected starter from StarterSelectScene must become the player's first active creature.Its data must persist into battle correctly.5. Registry state must be stableUse Phaser registry consistently for:- playerParty- playerCollection- currentEncounterPosition- playerName- selectedStarterBattle transitions must not wipe or corrupt this data.6. Encounter rules must stay simple and correct- Encounters only in Greenpaw Forest tall grass- No village encounters- Use encounter tables, not random hardcoded enemy creation- At least 3 forest creatures in the first encounter pool7. BattleScene must be readableAt minimum show:- player creature name- enemy creature name- player HP- enemy HP- battle log text- action menuThe screen can still use simple placeholder visuals, but it must be easy to understand.8. Action rules for this phaseSupport only:- Attack- Skill- Capture- RunKeep the first version simple and predictable.9. Enemy AI should be simple, not broken- Enemy should take a turn after the player unless battle already ended- Enemy does not need advanced tactics yet- But turn order must feel consistent10. Capture logic should be clear- Higher success chance at lower enemy HP- On success:  - add creature to collection  - show success message  - return to WorldScene- On failure:  - show failure message  - enemy gets its turn11. Return-to-world behavior must be correctAfter battle ends by:- victory- capture- runthe player must return to WorldScene:- on the same map- near the original encounter position- without losing registry state12. BattleScene should not become a giant file- Use battleSystem.js for calculations- Keep BattleScene focused on scene flow and UI- Keep code readable for a beginner13. 좋습니다. 지금 단계면 다음은 Phase 4로 가면 됩니다.
현재 확인 가능한 상태는 저장소가 JavaScript 기반으로 잡혀 있고, 아직 초기 커밋 단계이지만 Phaser 구조로 진행 중이며, 스크린샷상 탐험 → 야생 조우 → 전투 화면 진입까지는 연결된 상태입니다. 저장소도 JavaScript 중심입니다. 
이제 우선순위는 전투를 예쁘게 만드는 것보다, 전투 이후 상태가 게임 전체에 남도록 연결하는 것입니다.즉 다음 단계는:
포획 성공 시 컬렉션/파티에 저장
승리/도주 후 월드 복귀 안정화
도감(Codex) 최소 구현
첫 퀘스트 진행 연결
스타터 첫 진화 구조 심기
이 순서가 맞습니다.
아래 프롬프트를 그대로 보내세요.

지금 다음 단계에서 제일 중요한 건 **“전투가 끝나도 아무 일도 없던 것처럼 초기화되지 않게 만드는 것”**입니다.그 부분만 잡히면 이후 퀘스트, 진화, 도감은 훨씬 자연스럽게 붙습니다.
Feloria - Phase 4: Battle Persistence, Codex, Quests, and Evolution This phase shifts focus from isolated loops to persistent game state and long-term progression. The player will now be able to track their collection, follow a structured quest, level up their starter, and view their party through the game menu. Proposed Changes 💾 Persistence & Battle Rewards battleSystem.js : Add logic for calculating experience drops and handling level-ups/stat-increases. BattleScene.js : On battle end (victory/capture/run), explicitly update the playerParty array in the registry so HP and EXP modifications persist. creatures.js : Add baseExp yield for wild cats and an evolution object for starters (e.g., evolution: { target: 'BRAMBLECAT', level: 10 }). Level growth logic will be integrated into the battle end flow. 📖 Codex System [NEW] codex.js: A centralized data manager using the registry state arrays seenCreatureIds and caughtCreatureIds. Provide helper methods like markSeen(id) and markCaught(id). CodexScene.js : Implement as an overlay scene (similar to DialogScene but larger). It will list all species in creatures.js , revealing names and stats only if they exist in the registry arrays. Integration: Update BattleScene init to mark the enemy as seen. Update BattleScene capture success to mark enemy as caught. 🗺️ Quest System [NEW] quests.js: Data manager for the active quest log. First Quest ("First Steps"): Objective 1: Talk to Mira. (Triggered in WorldScene.handleInteraction) Objective 2: Choose Starter. (Triggered in StarterSelectScene ) Objective 3: Enter Forest. (Triggered in WorldScene create based on map ID) Objective 4: Trigger Encounter. (Triggered in BattleScene init ) Objective 5: Capture Cat. (Triggered in BattleScene capture success) Objective 6: Return to Mira. (Triggered in WorldScene.handleInteraction returning quest completion!) QuestScene.js : Overlay UI displaying current objectives and their completion status. 📱 Menu System MenuScene.js : An overlay UI triggered by pressing 'Esc' or 'Enter' in WorldScene . Buttons: Party: Opens PartyScene (displays current party condition). Codex: Opens CodexScene.js . Quests: Opens QuestScene.js . Close: Resumes exploration. Verification Plan Automated Tests npm run dev to verify the module imports and game bundle correctly. Manual Verification Registry & Battles: Fight a battle. Ensure the active party member's HP persists into the overworld and consecutive battles. Verify the player gains EXP after defeating an enemy. Codex: Encounter a Snagpuss. Open the menu -> Codex. Verify Snagpuss is marked as Seen but not Caught. Quests: Talk to Elder Mira in the village. Verify the quest objective completes in the Quest tab. Navigate to the forest and trigger an encounter, verifying subsequent objectives check off. Evolution: Manually set a starter's level to 9, win a battle to level up to 10, and verify the evolution log triggers (base system preparation).

Feloria - Phase 5: Leveling, Party Management, and EvolutionPhase 4 systems are working.Battle persistence, Codex tracking, and quest progression are functioning correctly.Now proceed to Phase 5.Goal:Introduce creature progression systems and party management.Scope for this phase:1. Experience and levelingWhen defeating a wild creature:- award EXP based on enemy baseExp- add EXP to the active creature- if EXP >= next level threshold:  - level up the creature  - increase stats  - show level up message2. Evolution systemSupport evolution conditions in creature data.Example:Leafkit -> Bramblecat (level 10)Emberpaw -> Cinderclaw (level 10)Misttail -> Dewtail (level 10)If a creature reaches its evolution level:- trigger evolution-ready state- optionally display a simple evolution messageFull evolution animation can be added later.3. Party managementExpand PartyScene functionality.Add:- view party member stats- switch active party order- add creature from collection to party- remove creature from partyKeep the maximum party size limited (for example 3 or 6).4. Collection integrationCaptured creatures must go into playerCollection.PartyScene must allow moving creatures between:- party- collection5. Battle integrationBattleScene must:- update EXP after victory- update party creature data- support evolution check after level up6. UI scopeUse simple readable UI for now.Do not attempt final polish yet.Focus on functionality.Verification targets:- defeating enemies grants EXP- EXP increases correctly- level up occurs- evolution condition can trigger- party order can change- captured creatures appear in collection- creatures can move between party and collection
개인적으로 평가
지금 Feloria 상태는 초기 프로토타입 기준으로 꽤 잘 진행된 상태입니다.
특히 잘된 점:
Phaser scene 구조
registry state 유지
encounter → battle → return loop
quest trigger 연결
codex tracking
이 5개가 초반 RPG에서 가장 어려운 부분입니다.
지금부터는 게임이 커지는 단계입니다.
원하시면 다음 답변에서 Feloria 프로젝트에서 앞으로 반드시 생길 버그 7개도 미리 알려드리겠습니다.(지금 미리 알면 개발 속도가 많이 빨라집니다.)
Feloria - Phase 5: Leveling, Party Management, and Evolution This phase focuses on creature progression and managing the player's team. We will polish the leveling system, implement the actual evolution state change, and build a robust PartyScene to organize captured creatures. Proposed Changes 📈 Leveling & Evolution battleSystem.js : Verify calculateExp and gainExp . When gainExp sets readyToEvolve = true, we need a new method evolveCreature(creature) that transforms the creature into its evolved form (e.g., Leafkit -> Bramblecat) by updating its id, name, base stats, and calculating its new current stats. BattleScene.js : After victory, if the creature leveled up and is readyToEvolve, trigger the evolveCreature method. Display an evolution message in the battle log before ending the battle. Make sure the updated evolved state is persisted to playerParty and playerCollection. 👥 Party Management & Collection PartyScene.js : Overhaul the scene to support interactivity. Party View: Show up to 3 creatures in the active party. Display full stats (HP, Attack, Defense, Level, EXP). Collection View: Show a scrollable list of creatures in playerCollection that are not currently in the active party. Actions: Click a party member to view options (e.g., "Make Active", "Remove from Party"). Click a collection member to view options (e.g., "Add to Party"). Constraints: Active creature (index 0) is the one sent into battle. "Make Active" swaps a creature to index 0. Max party size is 3. Cannot add more if full. Cannot remove the last creature from the party. 💾 Persistence Validation Ensure that modifying the party in PartyScene updates playerParty in the Phaser registry. When saving an evolved creature, ensure the actual instance reference in playerCollection is properly updated (or since playerParty items are references, they might update automatically, but we must verify). Verification Plan Automated Tests npm run dev to verify scene logic and UI rendering. Manual Verification Leveling & Evolution: Modify StarterSelectScene or a debug trigger to give the starter enough EXP to hit Level 10. Enter a battle, win, and observe the "Leafkit is evolving!" message. Return to the overworld and open the Party menu to verify the starter is now Bramblecat. Party Management: Capture 2-3 wild cats. Open Party Menu. Verify captured cats are either in the party (if space) or collection. "Remove from Party" to move a cat to the collection. "Add to Party" to move a cat from collection to party. "Make Active" to change the first cat. Enter battle and verify the new active cat is sent out. 이렇게 plan을 주네 아니그리고 반드시 생길 버그 7개가 안생기게끔 처음부터 알려줘야지
네, 플랜 방향은 맞습니다.다만 그대로 진행시키면 높은 확률로 터질 버그들이 있습니다. 그걸 먼저 막는 조건까지 같이 보내는 게 맞습니다.
아래 문구를 안티그래비티에 그대로 보내세요.플랜 승인 + Phase 5 진행 조건 + 미리 막아야 할 핵심 버그 방지 규칙까지 합친 버전입니다.
Approved — proceed with Phase 5.The direction is correct:- leveling- evolution- party management- collection management- persistence validationHowever, implement Phase 5 under the following constraints so common progression bugs do not appear.--------------------------------PHASE 5 GOAL--------------------------------The goal of this phase is:- real EXP gain after battle- level up- actual evolution state change- interactive PartyScene- stable transfer between party and collection- persistent registry updatesDo not expand into late-game systems yet.Focus on making progression stable.--------------------------------REQUIRED IMPLEMENTATION RULES--------------------------------1. Keep Phaser 3 + JavaScript- Do not switch to TypeScript- Do not reintroduce React gameplay components- Keep the current Phaser scene architecture2. Keep data-driven creature progressionUse creature data for:- id- name- level- exp- stats- evolution target- evolution levelDo not hardcode starter-only evolution logic inside BattleScene.3. Evolved creatures must become real updated creature objectsWhen evolution happens:- update id- update name- update base stats- recalculate max stats- preserve current level- preserve exp- preserve current HP proportion if possible- persist the evolved creature back into both playerParty and playerCollection correctly4. Party management must be safeRules:- maximum party size = 3- active creature is always index 0- cannot remove the last creature from party- add/remove between party and collection must never duplicate creatures- make active must swap order instead of cloning5. Registry remains the single source of truthUse Phaser registry consistently for:- playerParty- playerCollection- seenCreatureIds- caughtCreatureIds- playerName- selectedStarterDo not create disconnected local copies that are never written back.--------------------------------BUG PREVENTION RULES--------------------------------These bugs are likely to happen if not handled carefully.Prevent them from the start.BUG 1 — Duplicate creature entriesProblem:A captured or moved creature can appear in both party and collection multiple times.Prevent it by:- giving every creature instance a unique instanceId- moving instances between party and collection by instanceId- never clone on add/remove unless intentionally creating a new instance- before inserting, check whether that instanceId already exists in the target listBUG 2 — Evolution updates only one listProblem:A creature evolves in party but still shows old form in collection, or vice versa.Prevent it by:- updating the same creature instance consistently- or if immutable updates are used, update both playerParty and playerCollection using instanceId matching- never assume both arrays magically stay in syncBUG 3 — EXP/level up not persisting after battleProblem:BattleScene shows level up, but returning to WorldScene resets the creature.Prevent it by:- writing updated party data back into registry before ending battle- ensuring return-to-world flow reads the latest registry state- not keeping stale cached references in WorldSceneBUG 4 — Current HP becomes invalid after level up/evolutionProblem:HP goes above max HP, becomes negative, or resets unexpectedly.Prevent it by:- after stat recalculation, clamp currentHp to maxHp- preserve HP ratio if evolving, or at minimum clamp safely- always validate:  currentHp = Math.max(1, Math.min(currentHp, maxHp))  unless the creature actually faintedBUG 5 — PartyScene actions corrupt orderProblem:Make Active, Remove, and Add to Party can break party order or leave null/undefined slots.Prevent it by:- always rebuild party arrays cleanly after each action- validate party length after every mutation- ensure index 0 always exists if party is non-empty- never leave sparse arraysBUG 6 — Removing last party member soft-locks the gameProblem:Player ends up with no usable active creature and cannot enter battle correctly.Prevent it by:- block removing the final party member- if only one creature remains in party, disable Remove action- always validate party.length >= 1BUG 7 — Evolution triggers multiple timesProblem:A creature can re-trigger the same evolution repeatedly after every battle.Prevent it by:- after evolving, replace evolution metadata appropriately- clear readyToEvolve after evolution- ensure evolved form does not still meet the previous form’s trigger- evolution check should happen once per battle resolution, not repeatedly during UI updates--------------------------------PHASE 5 FUNCTIONAL REQUIREMENTS--------------------------------1. EXP and levelingAfter winning a battle:- award EXP using enemy baseExp- add EXP to active creature- level up if threshold reached- update stats- persist results2. EvolutionIf a creature reaches its evolution level:- trigger evolution-ready- perform actual evolution state change- show a readable evolution message in battle log- persist evolved form to registry3. PartyScene overhaulImplement:- Party View- Collection View- Add to Party- Remove from Party- Make ActiveRules:- max party size = 3- active creature = index 0- cannot remove last party creature4. Collection integrationCaptured creatures must go into collection.If party has room, they may also be placed into party according to the current design.But do not allow duplication bugs.--------------------------------VERIFICATION REQUIREMENTS--------------------------------Before moving to the next phase, verify all of the following:1. Winning a battle gives EXP2. EXP persists after returning to overworld3. Level up occurs correctly4. Evolution changes the actual creature form5. Evolved creature is correct in PartyScene6. Evolved creature is correct in Collection7. Captured creatures do not duplicate unexpectedly8. Add to Party works9. Remove from Party works10. Make Active works11. Active creature at index 0 is the one used in battle12. Last party member cannot be removed13. Party and collection remain valid after repeated operations--------------------------------FINAL NOTE--------------------------------The goal of Phase 5 is not polish.The goal is to make progression stable and prevent future state corruption.Proceed under these constraints.
그리고 말씀하신 부분도 맞습니다.원래는 “나중에 생길 버그”가 아니라 지금 단계에서 미리 방지 규칙을 같이 넣는 게 맞습니다.
그래서 앞으로는 새 phase 들어갈 때마다 이런 식으로 보시면 됩니다.

원하시면 다음엔 제가 Phase 6 들어가기 전에 반드시 체크해야 할 구조 점검표도 미리 만들어드리겠습니다.
두마리 만났고 한마리는 잡고 한마리는 죽였어. https://github.com/Evan-Yoon/Feloria 경험치바가 안보여서 경험치를 받았는지는 모르겠어. 그리고 체력이 없어서 10레벨까지 레벨업을 할 여유가 없어서 진화가 됐는지도 검증을 하지 못했어. 구현이 제대로 됐는지 코드 직접 보면서 다음 단계 어떻게 할지 확인해줘.
1m 9s 동안 생각함
스크린샷 기준으로는 Phase 5가 “부분 완료” 상태입니다.정확히 말하면:
Party 관리: 동작함
Quest 진행: 동작함
Codex seen/caught 집계: 동작함
EXP / 레벨업 / 진화: 화면만으로는 검증 불가, 코드도 GitHub 쪽 응답 제한 때문에 깊게 확인하지 못함
저장소 루트는 아직 정리 전 상태입니다. README가 기본 Vite 템플릿 그대로이고, 저장소 히스토리도 아주 초기 단계입니다. 
지금 스크린샷에서 확인되는 건 이렇습니다.
확인된 것
PartyScene
Make Active가 실제로 동작해서 Thistlefur를 맨 앞으로 올린 상태가 보입니다.
파티 수 제한도 2/3으로 표시됩니다.
따라서 파티 순서 변경 로직은 살아 있습니다.
Codex
Seen: 2 | Caught: 1로 보이므로, 한 마리 조우 + 한 마리 포획 + 다른 한 마리 처치가 도감 집계에 반영된 것으로 보입니다.
다만 이름/설명 해금 UI는 아직 숨김(???) 중심이라 MVP 수준입니다.
Quest
First Steps가 전부 체크되어 있으므로,
Mira 대화
스타터 선택
숲 진입
조우
포획
Mira 복귀흐름은 연결된 것으로 보입니다.
아직 검증 안 된 것
EXP 지급
Party 화면에 EXP 수치가 보이지만, “전투 후 증가했는지”는 스크린샷만으로 판단이 어렵습니다.
특히 스크린샷상 Emberpaw Lv 5 / EXP 0/250로 보인다면, EXP가 아직 적용되지 않았거나, 적용 후 초기화되는 버그가 있을 수 있습니다.
레벨업
레벨업 메시지, 스탯 증가, 다음 전투 반영 여부가 확인되지 않았습니다.
진화
10레벨 도달 자체를 못 했으니 아직 미검증입니다.
그래서 “구현되었다”고 보기엔 이릅니다.
또 한 가지 중요한 점은, 저장소 루트 기준으로는 아직 React + TypeScript + Vite 기본 README가 남아 있고, Phaser 프로젝트로 완전히 정리된 문서 상태는 아닙니다. 그래서 구조상도 아직 정리 단계라고 보는 게 맞습니다. 
판단
지금 상태를 단계로 나누면:
Phase 4: 사실상 완료
Phase 5: 절반 정도 완료
Party / Codex / Quest 쪽은 됨
EXP / 레벨업 / 진화는 검증용 장치가 없어서 아직 불확실
즉, 다음 단계는 바로 Phase 6로 가는 게 아니라, Phase 5.5: progression verification and debugging을 한 번 거치는 게 맞습니다.
아래 문구를 그대로 보내세요.
Feloria - Phase 5.5: EXP, Level-Up, Evolution Verification and Debug ToolsPhase 5 is only partially verified.The following systems appear to be working from the current build:- PartyScene active swap- basic collection / captured creature tracking- quest progression for First Steps- Codex seen/caught countsHowever, EXP gain, level-up persistence, and evolution are not yet verified in a reliable way.Do not move on to the next major feature phase yet.First add proper progression verification and debugging support.Goals for this phase:1. Confirm EXP is actually awarded after battle2. Confirm EXP persists after returning to WorldScene3. Confirm level-up works correctly4. Confirm evolution works correctly5. Add temporary debug tools to test progression quicklyRequired implementation:1. Visible EXP feedback- In BattleScene, after victory, show:  - EXP gained  - current EXP after gain  - whether level up happened- In PartyScene, clearly display:  - current level  - current EXP  - EXP needed for next level2. Debug progression controlsAdd temporary debug actions accessible only in development:- Give active creature +50 EXP- Give active creature +200 EXP- Set active creature to level 9- Fully heal active creatureThese can be simple temporary buttons or keyboard shortcuts.They do not need final UI polish.3. Level-up validationAfter EXP gain:- update level if threshold reached- update stats- persist changes back to registry- confirm updated values remain after scene transitions4. Evolution validationWhen a starter reaches evolution level:- trigger evolution message- replace creature with evolved form- update party and collection consistently- preserve correct level / EXP / HP rules- prevent repeated evolution triggering5. Add temporary battle result summaryAfter battle, before returning to WorldScene, show a short summary:- Victory / Capture / Run- EXP gained- Level up? yes/no- Evolution? yes/no6. Party / collection consistency checksEnsure:- no duplicate creature instance appears in both party and collection incorrectly- evolved creature form is reflected in both places if applicable- active creature at index 0 remains correct after battle updates7. 지금은 새 기능 추가보다 EXP / 레벨업 / 진화가 실제로 되는지 눈으로 확인 가능한 상태를 만드는 게 먼저입니다.
Feloria - Phase 5.5: Progression Verification & Debug Tools This phase focuses on ensuring that Phase 5's progression systems (EXP, Level Up, Evolution) are robust, visually confirmed by the player, and easily testable before moving on to new content. Proposed Changes 🔍 Visible Progression Feedback BattleScene.js : Create a custom UI summary panel that appears after the battle ends, but before returning to the WorldScene . It will display: Battle Result (Victory / Capture / Fled) EXP gained Total EXP now Whether a level up occurred Whether an evolution occurred PartyScene.js : Update the creature cards to explicitly show the required EXP for the next level (e.g., EXP: 30 / 50) so progress is mathematically clear. 🛠️ Debug Progression Controls PartyScene.js : Add temporary debug keyboard listeners accessible while the menu is open: Press 1: Give the active creature (Index 0) +50 EXP. Press 2: Give the active creature (Index 0) +200 EXP (force multi-level or instant evolution). Press 3: Set the active creature's level to 9 and EXP to 400 (pre-evolution state). Press 4: Fully heal the active creature. These controls will call the battleSystem.gainExp logic manually and refresh the UI to prove that stats and evolution checks work exactly as they would in battle. 💾 Safe Evolution Verification partySystem.js / Registry Flow: Validate that the evolveCreature transformation correctly updates both the array reference in playerParty and its mirrored form in playerCollection. Verification Plan Automated Tests npm run dev Manual Verification Targets Debug Controls: Open Party menu. Press 1 to see EXP hit 50, trigger a level up, and see stats increase. Evolution Test: Press 3 to reach Level 9. Press 1 to hit Level 10. Confirm it evolves to Bramblecat/Cinderclaw/Dewtail. Battle Summary: Fight a wild battle and win. A summary screen should pause the game for 3 seconds, displaying EXP gained, before returning to the WorldScene. Post-Battle Persistance: After returning from battle, open the Party menu. Verify the EXP gained from the summary screen is accurately reflected in the registry data. 아그리고 verification은 무조건 내가 진행할거야
좋습니다. 플랜 자체는 괜찮습니다.그리고 verification은 직접 하신다는 점도 맞게 반영해야 합니다.
즉, 안티그래비티에는 자동 검증이나 수동 검증을 대신하려 하지 말고,검증 가능한 상태와 디버그 도구만 만들어라고 명확히 지시하는 게 맞습니다.
아래 문구를 그대로 보내세요.
Approved — proceed with Phase 5.5.This phase should focus on making progression systems testable and visibly verifiable.Important:I will do all verification manually myself.Do not treat automated or manual verification as something you are responsible for completing.Your job is to implement the systems and provide the debug hooks and UI feedback needed so I can test them directly.Proceed under the following constraints:1. ScopeThis phase should only focus on:- visible EXP feedback- visible level-up feedback- visible evolution feedback- PartyScene debug controls- safe registry updates for evolved creatures- clear post-battle progression summaryDo not expand into new story content or new regions yet.2. PartyScene EXP visibilityUpdate PartyScene so each party creature clearly shows:- current level- current HP- current EXP- EXP needed for next levelThe goal is that I can look at the Party screen and immediately understand whether EXP was applied correctly.4. Keep debug tools clearly temporaryMark these debug controls as temporary development tools in code comments.They can remain for now, but should be easy to remove later.9. Deliverable qualityThe goal is not polish.The goal is that I can clearly test:- EXP gain- level-up- evolution- post-battle persistence- party/collection consistencyProceed under these constraints.
그리고 지금 말씀하신 포인트는 중요합니다.앞으로도 phase 진행할 때는 안티그래비티에게 “검증 완료했다고 말하지 말고, 내가 검증할 수 있게 만들어라”라고 계속 못 박는 게 좋습니다.
원하시면 다음 단계에서는 제가**“안티그래비티가 검증했다고 착각하지 못하게 하는 고정 문구”**도 짧게 만들어드리겠습니다.
https://github.com/Evan-Yoon/Feloria 다 잘 구현됐네. 다음 해야할일 알려줘
43s 동안 생각함
네, 지금 기준으로는 다음 단계로 넘어가도 됩니다.스크린샷상 확인되는 건 다음입니다.
진화: Emberpaw가 Cinderclaw Lv 10으로 바뀌어 있어서 진화 트리거 자체는 동작한 것으로 보입니다.
전투 결과 요약 패널: 승리 시 EXP Gained, Total EXP가 뜨고, 포획 시 별도 결과 패널도 뜹니다.
파티 화면: 진화 결과가 파티에 반영되어 있습니다.이 정도면 Phase 5.5의 핵심 목표는 통과로 봐도 됩니다.
저장소 자체는 아직 정리 전입니다. 루트에 dist, node_modules가 그대로 있고, README.MD도 아직 사실상 비어 있는 수준입니다. 
다만 한 가지는 꼭 다시 확인해 두시는 게 좋습니다.스크린샷상 파티는 1/3인데 Collection이 비어 보입니다. 사용자가 직접 한 마리 포획했다고 하셨으니, 다음 단계 들어가기 전에 포획한 개체가 party 또는 collection 중 어디에 저장되는지, 그리고 게임 재진입 후에도 유지되는지는 한 번만 더 확인해 두는 게 좋습니다. 이건 새 기능 전에 잡아두면 편합니다.
다음 단계 추천
이제는 시스템 추가보다 **“게임다운 흐름”**을 만드는 게 맞습니다.즉 Phase 6 = 첫 번째 실제 콘텐츠 확장으로 가면 됩니다.
우선순위는 이 순서가 좋습니다.
두 번째 지역/루트 추가
NPC 트레이너 배틀
회복 지점 / 상점
실제 도감 항목 표시 강화
월드 그래픽 정리
지금은 탐험-조우-전투-진화까지 코어 루프가 생겼으니, 다음부터는 “게임이 커지는 단계”입니다.
아래 프롬프트를 그대로 보내세요.
Feloria - Phase 6: First Real Content Expansion, Trainer Battles, Healing, Shop, and Better World ProgressionPhase 5.5 is good enough to move forward.The current project now has:- starter selection- world exploration- wild encounters- turn-based battle- capture- Codex / Quest / Party screens- level-up and starter evolution support- post-battle summary feedbackNow proceed to Phase 6.Goal:Turn the current prototype into a more game-like first chapter by adding real progression content beyond wild battles.Scope for this phase:1. Add a second real progression routeExpand the current world beyond the basic village/forest loop.Implement:- starwhisk_village- greenpaw_forest- mosslight_pathMosslight Path should act as the first route beyond the forest.2. Add trainer battlesIntroduce NPC trainer battles for the first time.Requirements:- at least 2 trainer NPCs- trainers initiate battle when interacted with- trainers should not be re-battleable after defeat unless explicitly designed- trainer battles should use party-style creature data, not wild encounter generation3. Add a healing systemImplement a basic healing point.Options:- Elder Mira heals partyor- a simple village healing station / innRequirements:- restore current HP for all party creatures- clear fainted state if applicable- save updated party state back to registry4. Add a shop systemImplement a very simple shop interaction in Starwhisk Village.Shop inventory for now:- Potion- Yarn BallRequirements:- simple currency system (gold/coins)- simple purchase UI or menu- inventory count increases after purchase- purchases persist through registry/state5. Inventory foundationIf not already present, implement a simple inventory system for:- healing items- capture itemsUse data files where possible.6. Codex improvementThe Codex should now show more than counts.For seen creatures:- show creature name- show habitat- show short descriptionFor caught creatures:- show additional details such as level seen or simple stat summary if appropriateDo not keep all seen creatures as only ??? if data is available.7. World progressionTie progression to actual gameplay:- complete First Steps- unlock Mosslight Path- trainer battle blocks path until defeated or spoken to- village healing/shop becomes meaningful before continuing onward8. Keep Phaser 3 + JavaScript- Do not switch to TypeScript- Do not reintroduce React gameplay components- Keep scene/data modularity9. Data organizationUse or expand separate data/modules for:- creatures- skills- encounters- trainers- items- inventory- shop inventory- quests- codexDo not hardcode all of this directly inside scenes.10. Verification-ready implementationDo not claim these systems are verified.Implement them so they can be tested manually.Key things that must be testable:- trainer battle starts and ends correctly- defeated trainer state persists- healing restores party correctly- shop purchases reduce currency and add items- inventory persists- Codex shows actual data for seen/caught creatures- progression from village -> forest -> route feels connected11. Cleanup / project hygieneAlso clean up obvious repository issues:- stop committing node_modules- stop committing dist- improve README- document controls and current game loopFinal note:The goal of Phase 6 is to make Feloria feel like a real early-game RPG chapter, not just a combat/system testbed.Prioritize trainer battles, healing, shop, and route progression before larger content expansion.
지금 시점에서의 추천 방향
지금부터는 새 시스템 10개를 한 번에 넣는 것보다,“첫 마을 → 첫 숲 → 첫 루트 → 첫 트레이너 → 회복/상점” 이 흐름을 완성하는 게 제일 좋습니다.
원하시면 다음에는 제가 Phase 6 들어가기 전에 꼭 확인해야 할 버그 방지 체크리스트도 같이 정리해드리겠습니다.
Feloria - Phase 6: First Real Content Expansion This phase transforms the isolated mechanics into a cohesive first chapter. We establish a functioning economy (shopping, healing), introduce NPC Trainer battles, expand the world to a new route, and improve the Codex to definitively reward exploration. Proposed Changes 🗺️ World Expansion (Mosslight Path) mapData.js / Map Loading: Create a new map definition mosslight_path with a collision layer, grass layer, NPC spawns, and a warp back to greenpaw_forest. WorldScene.js : Update warp logic in Greenpaw Forest to allow traversing to Mosslight Path once the First Quest is complete (or allow open exploration, dependent on design). ⚔️ Trainer Battles trainers.js [NEW]: Create a data file defining NPC trainers. Each trainer will have an id, name, dialogue (before/after), and a party array containing pre-defined creature configurations (species, level). WorldScene.js : Update handleInteraction to detect trainer NPCs. If a trainer is not yet defeated (tracked in registry.defeatedTrainers), trigger pre-battle dialogue, then start BattleScene with isTrainer: true and pass the trainer ID. BattleScene.js : Update logic to handle trainer parties. Instead of a single wild cat, the enemy is a list of cats. When one faints, send out the next. Disable capturing during trainer battles. Upon defeating all enemy cats, grant rewards (EXP, Gold) and mark the trainer as defeated in the registry. 🏥 Healing System WorldScene.js / dialogueSystem.js : Designate Elder Mira (or a dedicated bed/station) as the healing spot in Starwhisk Village. When interacted with, trigger a dialogue option "Heal Party?". If yes, iterate through registry.playerParty and set currentHp = maxHp. Play a sound/flash effect. Save party to registry. 💰 Shop and Inventory System items.js [NEW]: Define items like potion (restores HP) and capture_crystal. shopSystem.js [NEW]: Define the village shop inventory and prices. inventorySystem.js [NEW]: Handle adding/removing items from registry.playerInventory and tracking registry.playerGold. ShopScene.js [NEW]: A simple overlay UI for purchasing items using Gold. WorldScene Integration: Add a Shopkeeper NPC to Starwhisk Village that triggers the ShopScene. 📖 Codex Improvements CodexScene.js : Currently, unseen cats are ???. Approved — proceed with Phase 6.This scope is correct.Phase 6 should turn the current prototype into a more cohesive early-game RPG chapter.Important:I will do all verification manually myself.Do not claim that systems are verified.Your job is to implement them in a way that is testable and stable.Proceed under the following constraints.--------------------------------PHASE 6 GOAL--------------------------------The goal of this phase is to connect the current systems into a real early-game content loop by adding:- Mosslight Path- trainer battles- healing- shop + inventory + gold- Codex information expansionDo not add too many new regions yet.Keep the scope focused on the first chapter of the game.--------------------------------IMPLEMENTATION RULES--------------------------------1. Keep Phaser 3 + JavaScript- Do not switch to TypeScript- Do not reintroduce React gameplay components- Keep the current Phaser scene architecture2. Keep systems data-drivenUse separate files/modules for:- mapData- trainers- items- shopSystem- inventorySystem- dialogueSystemDo not hardcode everything directly inside WorldScene or BattleScene.3. Registry remains the single source of truthUse Phaser registry consistently for:- playerParty- playerCollection- playerInventory- playerGold- defeatedTrainers- currentMapId- seenCreatureIds- caughtCreatureIds- quest stateDo not create disconnected scene-local copies that fail to write back.4. Mosslight Path must be a real progression route- It must connect properly to Greenpaw Forest- Warp transitions must work both directions- It must contain at least one trainer and one wild encounter area- It should feel like a continuation of the first chapter, not just another placeholder map5. Trainer battles must differ from wild battles- Trainer battles use predefined parties from trainers.js- Trainer enemies can send out multiple creatures- Capturing must be disabled in trainer battles- After defeating a trainer, defeatedTrainers must update in registry- Re-interacting with defeated trainers must show post-battle dialogue instead of restarting battle6. Healing must actually update registry state- Healing must set currentHp = maxHp for all party creatures- If fainted state exists, it must be cleared as well- Updated party state must persist after leaving the healing interaction7. Shop and inventory must be real stateful systems- Buying an item must decrease gold- Buying an item must increase inventory count- Inventory and gold must persist in registry- Do not fake purchases with UI-only changes8. Codex must reveal meaningful data- unseen creatures stay hidden- seen creatures show:  - name  - habitat  - short description- caught creatures additionally reveal:  - base HP  - base ATK  - base DEFor equivalent simple stat info--------------------------------PHASE 6 BUG PREVENTION CHECKLIST--------------------------------Before and during implementation, guard against the following bugs.BUG 1 — Warp loops or bad spawn positionsProblem:Entering a warp can send the player back and forth instantly, or place them inside a blocking tile.Prevent it by:- defining explicit target spawn coordinates for each warp- validating that spawn coordinates are walkable- adding a short warp cooldown so the player does not instantly retrigger the destination warpBUG 2 — Trainer battle state not persistingProblem:A defeated trainer can still battle repeatedly because the defeat flag was not saved correctly.Prevent it by:- storing defeated trainer IDs in registry.defeatedTrainers- checking this state before starting a trainer battle- updating interaction dialogue after defeatBUG 3 — Multi-creature trainer battles breaking turn flowProblem:After one enemy creature faints, the next one may not load correctly, or battle may end too early.Prevent it by:- treating trainer parties as ordered arrays- moving to the next enemy only after faint resolution completes- only ending battle when the full trainer party is defeatedBUG 4 — Capture accidentally allowed in trainer battlesProblem:Player can still click Capture and recruit trainer-owned creatures.Prevent it by:- disabling or hiding Capture in trainer battles- guarding this rule in battle logic, not just UIBUG 5 — Healing updates UI but not actual dataProblem:Party appears healed in dialogue flow, but party data in registry still has old HP.Prevent it by:- explicitly writing healed party data back into registry- reopening PartyScene after healing should show full HPBUG 6 — Shop purchase changes UI onlyProblem:Gold or item count appears updated on screen but resets after scene changes.Prevent it by:- writing both playerGold and playerInventory back into registry immediately after each transaction- validating with scene reopen behaviorBUG 7 — Negative gold or invalid purchasesProblem:Player can buy items without enough gold or gold can go below zero.Prevent it by:- checking affordability before purchase- blocking purchase if playerGold < item price- clamping gold to non-negative valuesBUG 8 — Duplicate inventory entriesProblem:Buying the same item multiple times creates duplicate objects instead of increasing quantity.Prevent it by:- storing inventory as itemId -> quantity or equivalent normalized structure- increment quantity instead of pushing duplicate item objectsBUG 9 — Codex reveal logic inconsistentProblem:Seen/caught state updates counts but entry text remains hidden, or caught entry does not reveal more info.Prevent it by:- driving Codex display directly from seenCreatureIds and caughtCreatureIds- using consistent rules for what fields are visible at each discovery levelBUG 10 — Trainer reward persistence issuesProblem:Gold reward or EXP reward is shown after trainer battle but not saved.Prevent it by:- applying rewards to registry state before returning to WorldScene- ensuring post-battle summary reflects the saved values, not temporary onesBUG 11 — Party wipe or reference corruption after healing/shop/trainer flowProblem:A scene mutates party data incorrectly and party becomes empty, duplicated, or stale.Prevent it by:- always cloning/updating party arrays carefully- validating party length after every mutation- preserving the active creature at index 0 unless explicitly changedBUG 12 — Route progression blocked unintentionallyProblem:Player cannot access Mosslight Path because of a quest flag mismatch or missing unlock condition.Prevent it by:- choosing one clear rule:  either open path immediately  or unlock after First Steps quest completion- enforcing that rule consistently in one place--------------------------------PHASE 6 VERIFICATION-READY REQUIREMENTS--------------------------------Implement these so I can test them manually:1. Route integration- Village -> Forest -> Mosslight Path works- Mosslight Path -> Forest works- no broken warp loops2. Trainer battle flow- first interaction triggers trainer battle- capture is disabled- trainer can send multiple creatures if configured- defeated trainer does not restart battle on second talk3. Healing- damaged party returns to full HP after healing- Party screen reflects the healed values4. Shop / inventory / gold- buying Potion reduces gold- buying Capture Crystal reduces gold- inventory count increases correctly- values persist after scene transitions5. Codex reveal behavior- seen creatures show meaningful info- caught creatures show expanded info--------------------------------FINAL NOTE--------------------------------The goal of Phase 6 is not just adding more systems.The goal is to make the first chapter feel like a real RPG loop with:- route progression- trainer battles- healing- shopping- meaningful creature discoveryProceed under these constraints.

그래서 아래 문장을 플랜 밑에 그대로 추가해서 보내세요.
Phase 6 승인 + 필수 추가 조건
Approved — proceed with Phase 6.The plan is correct and aligned with the current architecture.However, the following additional constraints must be enforced to prevent state corruption and gameplay bugs during Phase 6 implementation.--------------------------------STATE CONSISTENCY RULES--------------------------------1. Registry must remain the single source of truth.All game state must be written to and read from the Phaser registry:- playerParty- playerCollection- playerInventory- playerGold- defeatedTrainers- seenCreatureIds- caughtCreatureIds- currentMapIdNo scene should maintain its own copy of these values without writing them back.--------------------------------WARP SAFETY RULES--------------------------------2. Warps must include explicit spawn coordinates.Each warp must define:- targetMapId- spawnX- spawnYWhen spawning the player after warp:- ensure the spawn tile is walkable- prevent immediate warp re-trigger by applying a short warp cooldown--------------------------------TRAINER BATTLE SAFETY--------------------------------3. Trainer battles must strictly differ from wild battles.Rules:- capture must be disabled- enemy creatures come from trainer.party- enemy creatures appear sequentially- battle ends only when trainer party is empty- trainer ID must be stored in registry.defeatedTrainers after victoryRe-interacting with defeated trainers must trigger post-battle dialogue instead of restarting battle.--------------------------------INVENTORY SAFETY--------------------------------4. Inventory must use normalized structure:playerInventory = {  potion: quantity,  capture_crystal: quantity}Never store duplicate item objects in arrays.When purchasing:- verify playerGold >= price- subtract gold- increase quantity- immediately write changes back to registryGold must never go below zero.--------------------------------HEALING SYSTEM SAFETY--------------------------------5. Healing must update registry state directly.When healing occurs:- set currentHp = maxHp for every creature in playerParty- persist updated party array back into registry- PartyScene must reflect healed values immediately after reopening.--------------------------------CODEX VISIBILITY RULES--------------------------------6. Codex entry visibility must depend strictly on discovery state.If creature is unseen:  show "???"If creature is seen:  show name + habitat + descriptionIf creature is caught:  show name + habitat + description + base statsThe display must be driven only by:- seenCreatureIds- caughtCreatureIds--------------------------------DELIVERABLE GOAL--------------------------------Phase 6 should result in a playable early chapter loop:Starwhisk Village→ Greenpaw Forest→ Mosslight Path→ Trainer battle→ Return to village→ Heal / Shop / Continue exploringThe focus is stable progression, not visual polish.
지금 플랜 기준 Phase 6에서 만들어지는 게임 구조
지금까지 시스템을 보면 Phase 6 끝나면 Feloria는 이렇게 됩니다.
Start ↓Village ↓Forest ↓Wild Battle ↓Capture / EXP / Level ↓Route (Mosslight Path) ↓Trainer Battle ↓Reward (Gold + EXP) ↓Village ├ Heal ├ Shop └ Codex
이 시점부터는 진짜 RPG 느낌이 나기 시작하는 단계입니다.
다음 Phase (미리 알려드림)
Phase 6 끝나면 다음은 보통 이 순서입니다.

하나만 추가로 말씀드리면
지금 Feloria 구조는 초기 인디 몬스터 RPG 구조로 굉장히 잘 잡힌 상태입니다.
특히 잘 된 점:
Phaser scene 구조
registry 기반 state
encounter → battle → return loop
codex tracking
quest triggers
party system
이 6개는 보통 처음 만들 때 제일 망가지기 쉬운 부분입니다.
원하시면 다음 답변에서**Feloria 프로젝트가 커질 때 반드시 생기는 “구조 붕괴 버그 5개”**도 미리 알려드리겠습니다.(이거 알면 프로젝트가 훨씬 오래 살아남습니다.)
트레이너 이기면 돈 주는데 일반 몹 죽이면 돈 소량으로 드랍이 되면 좋겠어. 그리고 아이템을 사는것은 되는데 아이템을 사용하는 곳은 못찾겠네. 촌장한테 말걸면 회복도 잘 되네. 그리고 트레이너랑 배틀해서 이기면 다시 대화해도 배틀 못하게 잘 막혀있어. https://github.com/Evan-Yoon/Feloria 여기서 코드 확인해주고 다음 해야할일 알려줘
17s 동안 생각함
지금 상태면 Phase 6은 의도한 방향으로 잘 들어갔다고 봐도 됩니다.
확인된 점은 이렇습니다.
저장소는 Phaser 기반 JS 프로젝트로 계속 진행 중이고, 현재 공개 저장소 기준 커밋 수는 아직 적지만 구조는 유지되고 있습니다. 다만 dist와 node_modules가 아직 저장소에 같이 올라가 있어 정리는 필요합니다. 
스크린샷상 트레이너 승리 보상이 정상적으로 들어갑니다. EXP Gained: +60 | Gold: +50가 표시되고, 레벨업과 진화 메시지도 함께 뜹니다.
일반 야생 배틀 보상도 EXP는 정상 표시됩니다. EXP Gained: +18, Total EXP: 77 / 500처럼 요약 패널이 잘 보입니다.
상점 구매도 동작합니다. Gold: 110 상태에서 Potion과 Capture Crystal을 살 수 있고, 구매 메시지도 뜹니다.
회복 시스템은 사용해 보신 대로 촌장 상호작용으로 잘 동작하고,
트레이너 재대결 방지도 잘 막혀 있는 상태입니다.
즉 현재는 Phase 6의 핵심인
Mosslight Path 확장
트레이너 배틀
healing
shop
Codex 확장
중에서 적어도 트레이너 보상 / 상점 / 회복 / 재대결 방지는 잘 잡힌 상태로 보입니다.
다만 지금 사용자님이 짚으신 두 가지가 바로 다음 우선순위입니다.
지금 바로 보강해야 할 것
첫째, 일반 몹도 소량의 골드 드랍을 주는 것.지금 스크린샷 기준으로는 트레이너만 골드를 주고, 야생은 EXP만 주는 구조로 보입니다.이건 게임 감각상 꽤 중요합니다.
추천은 이 정도입니다.
야생 전투 승리: +3 ~ +10 Gold
포획 성공: Gold 없음 또는 아주 소량
트레이너 승리: 지금처럼 더 큰 보상 유지
둘째, 아이템 사용 UI/플로우입니다.지금은 “사는 것”은 되지만 “쓰는 곳”이 없는 상태라 시스템이 반쪽입니다.이건 다음 단계에서 반드시 붙여야 합니다.
우선순위는:
PartyScene에서 Potion 사용
BattleScene에서 Capture Crystal 사용
필요하면 World 메뉴에서 Inventory 열기
다음 단계 추천
지금은 새 지역을 더 늘리기보다 아이템과 경제를 완성하는 게 맞습니다.즉 다음은 Phase 7: Inventory Usage, Wild Gold Drops, and Usable Item Flow가 좋습니다.
아래 프롬프트를 그대로 보내세요.
Feloria - Phase 7: Item Usage, Wild Gold Drops, and Inventory GameplayPhase 6 is in a good enough state to move forward.The current project now has:- world expansion into Mosslight Path- trainer battles- healing interaction- shop purchases- battle reward summaries- stable evolution / level-up feedback- defeated trainer persistenceNow proceed to Phase 7.Goal:Make the economy and inventory actually useful during gameplay.This phase should focus on:- wild enemy gold drops- usable healing items- usable capture items- visible inventory counts- inventory integration into battle and party managementImportant:I will do all verification manually myself.Do not claim systems are verified.Implement them in a way that is testable and stable.--------------------------------PHASE 7 FEATURES--------------------------------1. Wild battle gold dropsAdd a small gold reward for defeating normal wild creatures.Rules:- wild victories should grant a small amount of gold- trainer battles should still grant higher gold rewards- captured wild creatures may grant no gold or lower gold depending on design- gold reward must appear in the post-battle summarySuggested range:- wild battle victory: +3 to +10 Gold- trainer battle victory: keep current larger reward2. InventoryScene or usable inventory menuCreate a usable inventory interface.Requirements:- show current item quantities- show item descriptions- support selecting usable items- keep UI simple and readable3. Healing item usagePotion should be usable on party creatures.Requirements:- Potion restores HP- cannot heal above max HP- using Potion decreases quantity by 1- updated HP must persist to registry- if no Potions remain, usage must be blockedPreferred place to use:- PartySceneor- InventoryScene with target selection4. Capture item usage in battleCapture Crystal must be integrated into BattleScene.Requirements:- BattleScene should use the player's actual inventory quantity- using Capture Crystal consumes 1 item- cannot use it if quantity is 0- success/failure logic should remain tied to capture chance rules- trainer battles must still forbid capture item use5. Inventory persistenceRegistry must remain the single source of truth for:- playerInventory- playerGold- playerParty- playerCollectionNo scene-local fake inventory state.6. Inventory normalizationKeep inventory in normalized structure such as:playerInventory = {  potion: quantity,  capture_crystal: quantity}Do not store duplicate item objects in arrays.7. UI feedbackWhenever an item is used, show readable feedback:- "Potion used on Cinderclaw! +20 HP"- "Capture Crystal used!"- "No Potions left."- "Cannot capture a trainer's creature."8. Party integrationPartyScene should allow:- viewing party members- selecting a creature- using healing items on that creature9. Post-battle summary improvementBattle result summary should now include:- EXP gained- Gold gained- Total EXP- total Gold if convenient- level up message if triggered- evolution message if triggered10. Scope controlDo not add new maps or major story content in this phase.Focus only on making the current economy and items actually usable.--------------------------------BUG PREVENTION RULES--------------------------------1. Prevent negative item counts- item quantity can never go below 02. Prevent using items on invalid targets- Potion cannot be used on a non-existent creature- Potion cannot be used on creatures already at full HP unless explicitly allowed with no effect3. Prevent capture item use in trainer battles- disable or hide the option- also guard in logic, not just UI4. Prevent fake gold updates- gold changes must be written back to registry immediately- do not rely on temporary scene-only values5. Prevent inventory desync- shop purchases, battle item use, and party healing item use must all read/write the same playerInventory source--------------------------------MANUAL-TEST READY TARGETS--------------------------------Implement these so I can test them manually:- defeating a wild creature gives a small amount of gold- defeating a trainer still gives larger gold- buying items increases inventory count- Potion can be used from a menu on a party creature- Potion decreases by 1 when used- HP is restored correctly and persists- Capture Crystal decreases by 1 when used in battle- Capture Crystal cannot be used if quantity is 0- Capture Crystal cannot be used in trainer battles- post-battle summary shows both EXP and Gold where appropriateFinal note:The goal of Phase 7 is to make items, gold, and inventory part of the real gameplay loop instead of just supporting systems.
추가로 지금 시점에서 꼭 하셔야 하는 정리 하나는 있습니다.dist와 node_modules는 저장소에서 빼는 게 맞습니다. 공개 저장소 루트에 둘 다 보입니다. 
원하시면 다음에는 제가 .gitignore에 바로 넣을 내용까지 정리해드리겠습니다.
Feloria - Phase 7: Economy and Items Action Phase 7 shifts the focus from simply hoarding resources to actually consuming them to prolong the exploration loop. Proposed Changes 💰 Wild Gold Drops battleSystem.js : Add a new function calculateGold(enemyCat, isTrainer = false). Wild encounters will randomly roll between +3 and +10 Gold. Trainers will statically return their defined bounties. BattleScene.js : Update the victory() routine to dynamically fetch the required Gold payload using the new function, ensuring wild grinding still provides an economic drip. 🎒 Battle Item Consumption BattleScene.js : Update playerCapture() . Fetch playerInventory.capture_crystal from the registry. If quantity is < 1, block the action with a UI message: "Not enough Capture Crystals!" If > 0, deduct 1 and strictly write it back to the Registry before executing the capture roll. 🏥 Inventory Scene and Healing Items inventorySystem.js: We will formally ensure useItem(registry, itemId, targetCreature) exists to encapsulate the logic: Check if inventory has > 0 of the item. Check if the item is a Healing type (like potion). Attempt to use it (Potions fail if currentHp === maxHp). Decrease count and write back. InventoryScene.js [NEW]: Create an overlay scene similar to ShopScene . Reads the ITEMS database alongside playerInventory keys to display owned items and quantities. Selecting a potion will transition to a mini-Party select view (or jump directly to PartyScene in an "item target mode") to apply the heal. MenuScene.js : Add an "Inventory" button to the pause menu, taking the player to the new InventoryScene . Verification Plan Wild Battles: Enter the forest grass. Defeat a cat. Prove the battle summary awards +3 to +10 Gold. Item Count Block: From 0 crystals, try to capture a cat. It must fail. Walk to the shop, buy 2 crystals. Return to a battle, capture a cat. Check inventory: 1 crystal must remain. Healing Usage: Take battle damage. Open the Menu -> Inventory. Click a Potion, select the damaged cat. Verify HP increases, Potion count decreases by 1, and no negative numbers exist if repeatedly spammed.

메뉴에서 Inventory 진입

Approved — proceed with Phase 7.The direction is correct.This phase should make gold and items part of the actual gameplay loop.Important:I will do all verification manually myself.Do not claim anything is verified.Your job is to implement the systems so they are stable and directly testable.Proceed under the following constraints.--------------------------------PHASE 7 GOAL--------------------------------The goal of this phase is to make:- wild gold drops- usable inventory- healing item usage- capture item consumptionfeel like real gameplay systems instead of passive data.Do not add major new content or maps in this phase.Keep the scope focused on economy and item usage.--------------------------------IMPLEMENTATION RULES--------------------------------1. Keep Phaser 3 + JavaScript- Do not switch to TypeScript- Do not reintroduce React gameplay components- Keep the current Phaser scene structure2. Registry must remain the single source of truthAll item, gold, and party state must be read from and written back to Phaser registry:- playerInventory- playerGold- playerParty- playerCollectionNo scene-local fake inventory state.3. Wild gold dropsAdd small gold rewards for wild battle victories.Rules:- wild victory gives random +3 to +10 Gold- trainer battle reward logic remains separate- gold amount must appear in the battle summary- captured wild battles may give no gold or reduced gold according to final design, but the rule must be explicit and consistent4. Summary feedbackBattle result summary should clearly show:- battle result- EXP gained- Gold gained- total EXP if available- level up if triggered- evolution if triggered--------------------------------BUG PREVENTION RULES--------------------------------BUG 1 — Negative inventory countsPrevent item quantity from ever going below 0.BUG 2 — Consuming item on failed usability checkIf Potion is used on a full HP creature, do NOT consume the item.BUG 3 — Capture Crystal deducted but capture not attempted correctlyOnly deduct 1 crystal once per use attempt.Do not double-deduct on repeated clicks or scene updates.BUG 4 — Gold updated in summary but not savedGold changes must be written back to registry before leaving BattleScene.BUG 5 — Wild and trainer gold reward logic mixing togetherKeep trainer reward logic separate from wild reward logic.Do not accidentally apply both.BUG 6 — Inventory desync between shop and battleShop purchases, battle item use, and healing item use must all read and write the same normalized playerInventory structure.BUG 7 — Invalid item target handlingDo not allow Potion use on missing/null creatures.Do not allow target selection to create undefined behavior.BUG 8 — Repeated input causing duplicate consumptionGuard against button spam or repeated click events so one action only consumes one item.--------------------------------DATA STRUCTURE RULES--------------------------------Inventory should stay normalized, for example:playerInventory = {  potion: quantity,  capture_crystal: quantity}Do not store duplicate item objects in arrays.--------------------------------MANUAL-TEST READY TARGETS--------------------------------Implement these so I can test them manually:1. Defeating a wild creature gives +3 to +10 Gold2. Defeating a trainer still gives trainer-style larger Gold reward3. Battle summary shows Gold reward clearly4. Capture fails if no Capture Crystals remain5. Buying crystals from the shop increases quantity correctly6. Using a crystal in battle decreases quantity by exactly 17. Potion can be used from Inventory8. Potion heals the selected creature correctly9. Potion is not consumed if used on a full HP creature10. Inventory values persist after closing and reopening scenes--------------------------------FINAL NOTE--------------------------------The goal of Phase 7 is not polish.The goal is to make items, inventory, and gold reliable gameplay systems that are safe from duplication, desync, and invalid consumption bugs.Proceed under these constraints.

Phase 8: Save/Load, State Restoration, and Real Persistence
왜 이게 다음이냐면, 지금부터는 저장해야 할 상태가 많습니다.
playerParty
playerCollection
playerInventory
playerGold
seen / caught
quests
defeatedTrainers
currentMapId
player position
evolved starter state
이걸 저장 없이 계속 확장하면 나중에 구조가 쉽게 꼬입니다.
아래 프롬프트를 그대로 보내세요.
Feloria - Phase 8: Save/Load, State Restoration, and Persistent ProgressPhase 7 is in a good enough state to move forward.The current game now has:- exploration- wild battles- trainer battles- capture- leveling- evolution- healing- shop purchases- basic codex- quest progression- gold rewardsNow proceed to Phase 8.Goal:Add reliable save/load functionality so the current game state can persist across sessions and future content expansion remains stable.Important:I will do all verification manually myself.Do not claim anything is verified.Implement the systems so they are stable and easy to test.--------------------------------PHASE 8 GOAL--------------------------------This phase should add:- manual save- continue/load from title- autosave on important progression events- full state restoration into the current Phaser architectureDo not add new regions or large new gameplay systems in this phase.Focus on persistence and stability.--------------------------------SAVE / LOAD REQUIREMENTS--------------------------------1. Add save systemImplement a saveSystem.js or equivalent module.Use localStorage for now.Support at minimum:- one active save slot- save timestamp- save version number2. Save data contentsThe save file must include all important gameplay state:- playerName- selectedStarter- playerParty- playerCollection- playerInventory- playerGold- seenCreatureIds- caughtCreatureIds- active quests / completed quests- defeatedTrainers- currentMapId- player position / spawn coordinates- story flags if any- current starter evolution state- current levels / EXP / HP3. Continue optionThe Continue option on StartScene must now become functional.Rules:- if no save exists, Continue should be disabled or show "No save data"- if save exists, Continue should restore the saved game correctly- loading should return the player to the correct map and position4. Manual save accessAdd a simple Save option to the pause menu.Menu should now include:- Party- Inventory- Codex- Quests- Save- Close5. Autosave triggersAdd autosave after important events such as:- capturing a creature- defeating a trainer- making a shop purchase- healing the party- evolution- completing a quest step- changing mapsKeep autosave simple and reliable.6. Load behaviorWhen loading:- restore registry state from save data- restore current map- restore player position- restore party HP / EXP / evolution state- restore inventory and gold- restore defeated trainer status- restore codex progress- restore quest progressDo not partially load state.--------------------------------BUG PREVENTION RULES--------------------------------1. Prevent corrupted save crashes- if save data is missing fields, fall back safely- use a save version field- validate required keys before loading2. Prevent stale registry state- loading must overwrite active registry state fully- do not mix old session state with loaded state3. Prevent save/load desync- shop, battle, codex, quest, and party scenes must all read/write the same registry-backed state- save should serialize the source of truth, not scene-local temporary values4. Prevent bad spawn loads- saved player position must be restored only to valid walkable tiles- if position is invalid, fall back to a safe map spawn point5. Prevent defeated trainer reset- defeatedTrainers must persist correctly across reloads6. Prevent evolution rollback- evolved creature forms must remain evolved after saving and loading7. Prevent inventory/gold rollback- purchases and item consumption must persist after reload--------------------------------MANUAL-TEST READY TARGETS--------------------------------Implement these so I can test them manually:1. Save from menu2. Close/reload the game and Continue from title3. Return to the same map and position4. Party HP/EXP remain correct after reload5. Evolved creature remains evolved after reload6. Inventory and Gold remain correct after reload7. Captured creatures remain in collection after reload8. Defeated trainers stay defeated after reload9. Quest progress remains correct after reload--------------------------------FINAL NOTE--------------------------------The goal of Phase 8 is not visual polish.The goal is to make Feloria persistent and safe to expand.Do not move on to large new content until save/load is stable.
그리고 이 단계 끝나면 그다음은 보통 이 순서가 좋습니다.

story flags if any
current starter evolution state
current levels / EXP / HP
Continue optionThe Continue option on StartScene must now become functional.
Rules:
if no save exists, Continue should be disabled or show "No save data"
if save exists, Continue should restore the saved game correctly
loading should return the player to the correct map and position
Manual save accessAdd a simple Save option to the pause menu.
Menu should now include:
Party
Inventory
Codex
Quests
Save
Close
Autosave triggersAdd autosave after important events such as:
capturing a creature
defeating a trainer
making a shop purchase
healing the party
evolution
completing a quest step
changing maps
Keep autosave simple and reliable.
Load behaviorWhen loading:
restore registry state from save data
restore current map
restore player position
restore party HP / EXP / evolution state
restore inventory and gold
restore defeated trainer status
restore codex progress
restore quest progress
Do not partially load state.
Bug Prevention Rules
Prevent corrupted save crashes
if save data is missing fields, fall back safely
use a save version field
validate required keys before loading
Prevent stale registry state
loading must overwrite active registry state fully
do not mix old session state with loaded state
Prevent save/load desync
shop, battle, codex, quest, and party scenes must all read/write the same registry-backed state
save should serialize the source of truth, not scene-local temporary values
Prevent bad spawn loads
saved player position must be restored only to valid walkable tiles
if position is invalid, fall back to a safe map spawn point
Prevent defeated trainer reset
defeatedTrainers must persist correctly across reloads
Prevent evolution rollback
evolved creature forms must remain evolved after saving and loading
Prevent inventory/gold rollback
purchases and item consumption must persist after reload
Manual-Test Ready Targets
Implement these so I can test them manually:
Save from menu
Close/reload the game and Continue from title
Return to the same map and position
Party HP/EXP remain correct after reload
Evolved creature remains evolved after reload
Inventory and Gold remain correct after reload
Captured creatures remain in collection after reload
Defeated trainers stay defeated after reload
Quest progress remains correct after reload
Final Note
The goal of Phase 8 is not visual polish.The goal is to make Feloria persistent and safe to expand.
Do not move on to large new content until save/load is stable.

아 아니야 내 컴퓨터가 문제였네 이제 위에 잘보여. 원래 해주던대로 해줘.

Feloria - Phase 9: Visual Upgrade, Tilesets, Sprites, and UI CleanupPhase 8 is complete enough to move forward.The current game now has:- save/load- exploration- wild battles- trainer battles- capture- leveling- evolution- healing- shop purchases- inventory- codex- quest progression- persistent stateNow proceed to Phase 9.Goal:Replace placeholder visuals with a real pixel-art presentation so the game starts to feel like an actual monster-taming RPG instead of a systems prototype.Important:I will do all verification manually myself.Do not claim anything is verified.Implement the systems so they are stable and easy to test.--------------------------------PHASE 9 GOAL--------------------------------This phase should focus on:- overworld tileset rendering- player sprite rendering- NPC sprite rendering- battle monster sprite rendering- UI cleanup- clearer visual identity for FeloriaDo not add large new story content or many new regions in this phase.Focus on visual upgrade and presentation quality.--------------------------------VISUAL REQUIREMENTS--------------------------------1. Overworld tilesetsReplace simple placeholder map blocks with a consistent tileset-based overworld.Apply this first to:- starwhisk_village- greenpaw_forest- mosslight_pathRequirements:- real ground tiles- path tiles- grass / tall grass tiles- trees / bushes / rocks- village structures- route decorationKeep the existing map logic intact.Do not break collision, warps, or encounter zones while replacing visuals.2. Player spriteReplace the current placeholder player block with a proper top-down player sprite.Requirements:- idle frame- walking frames- directional facing if possible- consistent scale with tile size3. NPC spritesReplace placeholder NPC markers/blocks with readable NPC sprites.At minimum:- Elder Mira- Shopkeeper- Forest Explorer- Route trainers4. Battle spritesReplace battle placeholder blocks with actual monster battle sprites.Requirements:- player creature front/back presentation as appropriate- enemy creature sprite- correct sprite changes after evolution- readable positioning and scaleIf full unique art is not available yet, use consistent placeholder creature sprites instead of colored blocks.5. UI cleanupClean up the following scenes:- BattleScene- MenuScene- PartyScene- CodexScene- QuestScene- ShopScene- InventorySceneRequirements:- cleaner spacing- better text hierarchy- clearer buttons- consistent color palette- less prototype-like presentation6. Visual consistencyChoose one coherent visual style.Do not mix wildly different placeholder styles.--------------------------------TECHNICAL RULES--------------------------------1. Keep Phaser 3 + JavaScript- Do not switch to TypeScript- Do not reintroduce React gameplay components2. Asset organizationCreate or clean up local asset folders such as:- assets/tilesets- assets/sprites/player- assets/sprites/npcs- assets/sprites/creatures- assets/ui3. Preload all assets properlyUse PreloadScene to load tilesets, sprites, and UI graphics.Do not hardcode ad-hoc image creation where real assets now exist.4. Preserve gameplay behaviorVisual upgrades must not break:- save/load- battle flow- party state- quest progression- inventory- codex- trainer defeat persistence--------------------------------BUG PREVENTION RULES--------------------------------1. Do not break collision while changing map visuals2. Do not break encounter zones while replacing tall grass visuals3. Do not break trainer/NPC interactions when swapping sprites4. Do not break evolved creature identity when assigning battle sprites5. Do not introduce visual-only scene state that overrides registry-backed gameplay state--------------------------------MANUAL-TEST READY TARGETS--------------------------------Implement these so I can test them manually:1. Save/load still works after visual refactor--------------------------------PROJECT CLEANUP--------------------------------Also clean up basic repository hygiene:- stop committing node_modules- stop committing dist- improve README with current controls and gameplay loop--------------------------------FINAL NOTE--------------------------------The goal of Phase 9 is to make Feloria look like a real game while preserving the systems already built.Do not move on to major new content until the current prototype is visually coherent.

Phase 9: Visual Upgrade, Tilesets, Sprites, and UI Cleanup The objective of this phase is to replace the functional prototype blocks with consistent pixel-art visuals, making the game feel like a complete RPG. Proposed Changes 1. Project Organization & Hygiene Asset Folders: Create structured asset directories (assets/tilesets, assets/sprites/player, assets/sprites/npcs, assets/sprites/creatures, assets/ui). Git Hygiene: Add .gitignore to prevent committing node_modules and dist. Documentation: Update README.md to reflect current Phase 8 & 9 features, controls, and gameplay loop. 2. Asset Preloading Modify PreloadScene.js to load all new image resources from the new directory structure, replacing the dynamic graphics generation logic for player/NPC/monsters where applicable. 3. Maps & Tilesets Procure or generate a coherent RPG tileset (grass, paths, trees, buildings, water). Update the map generation/loading logic in mapLoader.js and WorldScene.js to consume Tiled JSON or configure tilemaps using Phaser's Tilemap API natively, rather than drawing rectangles. Apply to starwhisk_village, greenpaw_forest, and mosslight_path. Constraint: Preserve existing grid dimensions, collision layer logic, warp zones, and encounter zones. 4. Sprites Player: Generate a basic 4-directional sprite sheet. Update WorldScene.js and input handling to animate walking. NPCs: Generate varied NPC sprites (Elder Mira, Shopkeeper, Trainers) and replace their colored block rendering. Creatures (Combat): Replace colored blocks in BattleScene.js with consistent battle sprites representing the creatures (front view for enemy, back/side view for player). Apply logic to load evolved variants correctly. 5. UI Cleanup Refine layout, typography, and spacing in: BattleScene.js (cleaner health bars, better text boxes) MenuScene.js & StartScene.js & SaveLoadScene.js PartyScene.js & InventoryScene.js (better lists, clearer active selections) CodexScene.js & QuestScene.js ShopScene.js User Review Required IMPORTANT Since we are entering a heavy art phase, I will generate consistent baseline assets (tilesets, simple sprites). If you have specific art styles or reference images you want me to use, let me know! Otherwise, I will proceed with creating a standard retro pixel-art aesthetic. Verification Plan Manual Verification You will need to walk around the village, forest, and paths to verify map logic and collision are unbroken while observing the new tilesets. Talk to NPCs and engage in a wild battle to see the new character and creature sprites. Open all menus (Shop, Party, Codex, Save) to verify the UI cleanup. plan은 이렇다는데 나는 monster들이 고양이 느낌이면 좋겠어
좋습니다. 지금 나온 Phase 9 plan 자체는 괜찮습니다.다만 지금 중요한 건 아트 방향을 먼저 못 박는 것입니다.지금 말 안 하면 AI가 보통 generic 몬스터를 만들어버립니다.
사용자님이 원하는 건:
monster = 고양이 기반 creature
이걸 지금 반드시 명확히 지시해야 합니다.
그래서 plan에 아트 스타일 규칙을 추가해서 보내는 게 좋습니다.
아래 문장을 그대로 붙여서 보내세요.
Phase 9 추가 아트 방향 지시
Additional Art Direction RequirementAll creatures in Feloria must be cat-themed.Do not generate generic monsters.Design rules:1. Every creature must clearly resemble a cat or feline.Examples:- forest cat- flame cat- water cat- shadow cat- snow lynx- wild kitten- jungle cat2. Creature anatomy must remain feline:- ears- tail- whiskers- paw structure- cat body proportions3. Evolution lines must keep the feline identity.Example:Leafkit → BramblecatEmberpaw → CinderclawMisttail → DewtailSnagpuss → ThistlefurThe evolved forms should look like larger or more powerful cats,not completely different animals.4. Battle sprites should follow RPG creature presentation rules:- enemy creature: front-facing sprite- player creature: back or angled sprite- consistent sprite scale- readable silhouette5. Visual toneStyle should resemble:- classic handheld monster RPG pixel art- 16-bit era pixel style- clear outlines- limited but vibrant color palettesAvoid:- hyper realistic animals- chibi proportions that break combat readability- non-feline monster shapes6. NPCsNPCs must look human-like but exist in a world where cats are the creatures being trained.Example NPCs:- Elder Mira- Shopkeeper- Forest Explorer- Route Trainers7. Tileset toneVillage and forest maps should feel cozy and natural:Starwhisk Village- wooden houses- small paths- grass- fences- flowersGreenpaw Forest- trees- bushes- tall grass- mossMosslight Path- rocky trail- forest edges- trainer spots8. Maintain visual consistencyAll sprites must follow the same pixel-art scale and palette style.Do not mix different art styles.

지금 Feloria는 고양이 게임이기 때문에,아예 creature 디자인 방향도 미리 정해두는 게 좋습니다.

Feloria Cat Creature Design Pack Prompt
Feloria - Creature Design Pack (Cat-Based Monsters)All monsters in Feloria must be feline-based creatures.This is a strict design rule.Do NOT generate generic monsters or creatures based on random animals.Every monster must clearly resemble a cat or feline species.--------------------------------CREATURE DESIGN RULES--------------------------------All creatures must follow these anatomical rules:- cat ears- whiskers- tail- paw structure- feline body posture- recognizable cat silhouetteEvolution lines must preserve the feline identity.Evolved forms should feel like stronger or larger versions of the base cat.Avoid:- dragons- reptiles- insects- humanoid monsters- non-feline silhouettes--------------------------------VISUAL STYLE--------------------------------Use classic pixel-art RPG creature design principles.Style target:- retro handheld RPG- 16-bit pixel art- strong silhouette- readable color palettes- simple animation framesBattle sprites must support:Enemy creature- front-facing spritePlayer creature- back-facing or angled sprite--------------------------------CREATURE DATA STRUCTURE--------------------------------Each creature definition must include:- id- name- type- evolution- habitat- base stats (hp, attack, defense)- short codex description--------------------------------CREATURE TYPES--------------------------------Feloria creature types:- Forest- Fire- Water- Shadow- Rock- Ice- Storm- Spirit- Grass- Mystic--------------------------------STARTER CREATURES--------------------------------LeafkitType: ForestEvolution: Bramblecat (Lv10)EmberpawType: FireEvolution: Cinderclaw (Lv10)MisttailType: WaterEvolution: Dewtail (Lv10)--------------------------------FOREST CREATURES--------------------------------1. 원하시면 다음 답변에서**Feloria 게임을 훨씬 좋아 보이게 만드는 “UI 디자인 규칙 프롬프트”**도 만들어 드리겠습니다.
NPC는 사람이어야하는데 NPC조차 고양이로 바꿔버렸어.. 사람으로 만들어야해. 그리고 내 캐릭터가 안보여
맞습니다. 이건 아트 방향이 잘못 적용된 상태입니다.
지금 문제는 2가지입니다.
고양이 테마 규칙이 NPC까지 잘못 확장됨→ 고양이인 건 몬스터/크리처만이어야 합니다.→ NPC는 사람이어야 합니다.
플레이어 캐릭터 가시성 문제→ 플레이어 스프라이트가 없거나, 맵/배경과 구분이 안 되거나, 렌더 순서/좌표가 잘못된 상태입니다.
지금 바로 안티그래비티에 아래 문구를 그대로 보내세요.
The visual direction was applied incorrectly.Correction:Only the creatures/monsters in Feloria should be cat-themed.NPCs must be human characters.The player character must also be a human explorer and must be clearly visible in the overworld.Please fix the visual implementation under these exact rules.--------------------------------ART DIRECTION CORRECTION--------------------------------1. Creature rule- Only battle creatures / collectible monsters are cat-based.- Starters such as Leafkit, Emberpaw, Misttail remain feline creatures.- Wild creatures and evolved creatures remain feline creatures.2. NPC rule- NPCs must be human characters, not cats.- This includes:  - Elder Mira  - Shopkeeper  - Forest Explorer  - Route Trainers  - any village or route NPCs3. Player rule- The player must be a human adventurer/explorer.- The player must be clearly visible on the map at all times.- The player sprite must not blend into the terrain.- The player sprite must render above the map correctly.--------------------------------IMPLEMENTATION REQUIREMENTS--------------------------------1. Replace cat-like NPC sprites with human pixel spritesCreate or use simple human retro pixel sprites for NPCs.2. Add a proper visible player sprite- human sprite- readable silhouette- different enough from NPCs and terrain- correct layering / depth- proper spawn visibility3. Keep creatures cat-themed only where appropriate- starter select creature art stays cat-themed- battle creatures stay cat-themed- codex creature art stays cat-themed4. Preserve gameplayDo not break:- NPC interaction- battle flow- save/load- collision- warps- codex- quests--------------------------------VISUAL SAFETY RULES--------------------------------1. Player visibility- ensure player sprite is not hidden behind tiles by mistake- ensure player render depth is correct- ensure player spawn position is valid and visible- ensure player color palette contrasts with ground tiles2. NPC readability- NPCs should look human and distinct from monsters- NPCs should not be mistaken for wild creatures or player3. Role separationUse this visual rule consistently:- Player = human- NPCs = human- Monsters/Creatures = feline monstersDo not blur these categories.--------------------------------SPECIFIC FIX TARGETS--------------------------------Please fix at minimum:- StarterSelectScene creature visuals stay as cat creatures- WorldScene NPCs become human sprites- WorldScene player becomes a visible human sprite- Trainer NPCs become human sprites- BattleScene creatures remain cat creatures--------------------------------FINAL NOTE--------------------------------The current implementation misunderstood the art direction.Feloria is a world where humans interact with feline monsters.It is NOT a world where all NPCs are cats.Please correct this immediately before continuing further visual work.

Phase 10 프롬프트 (그대로 보내기)
Feloria - Phase 10: First Boss Chapter and New Region ExpansionThe current Feloria project has reached a stable gameplay foundation.Existing systems include:- exploration- wild encounters- trainer battles- capture mechanics- leveling and evolution- healing- shop and inventory- codex- quest progression- save/load- visual overworld tiles and spritesNow proceed to Phase 10.Goal:Create the first real story chapter and boss challenge.--------------------------------PHASE 10 FEATURES--------------------------------1. New mapsAdd two new connected maps:Ancient ForestMosslight ShrineThese should connect to the existing map progression:Starwhisk Village→ Greenpaw Forest→ Mosslight Path→ Ancient Forest→ Mosslight ShrineAncient Forest:- dense forest map- stronger wild creatures- trainer encountersMosslight Shrine:- small sacred ruin- boss battle location2. First Boss TrainerAdd a boss trainer or guardian battle in Mosslight Shrine.Example:Name: Guardian RowanParty example:- Mosslynx Lv12- Thornmane Lv14Boss battles should:- use trainer battle logic- reward large EXP and Gold- trigger story dialogue after victory3. Boss rewardAfter defeating the boss:Give the player a special reward such as:Forest BadgeorAncient RelicThis reward should unlock further world progression.4. New creature additionsAdd several new feline creatures tied to the forest region.Examples:Thornkit → Thornmane  Mosslynx → Verdantlynx  Vinefang  These creatures should appear in Ancient Forest encounters.5. Quest progressionAdd a new quest after "First Steps":Quest: Forest AwakeningObjectives:- Explore Mosslight Path- Enter Ancient Forest- Defeat Guardian Rowan at Mosslight ShrineCompleting the quest unlocks the next region.--------------------------------CONSTRAINTS--------------------------------Do not break existing systems.Ensure compatibility with:- save/load- party system- codex tracking- evolution- inventory- trainer defeat persistence--------------------------------MANUAL TEST TARGETS--------------------------------The following must be testable:- new maps load correctly- warps between all maps work- new creatures appear in encounters- boss battle starts correctly- defeating boss grants reward- quest updates after boss defeat- save/load preserves boss completion state--------------------------------FINAL NOTE--------------------------------The goal of Phase 10 is to turn Feloria from a sandbox prototype into the first real playable chapter of the game.
